
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Customer] (
    [CustomerNum]  INT            NOT NULL,
    [Name]         NVARCHAR (50)  NULL,
    [Email]        NVARCHAR (50)  NULL,
    [PhoneNum]     NVARCHAR (20)  NULL,
    [Address]      NVARCHAR (100) NULL,
    [CreditStatus] NVARCHAR (20)  NULL,
    [CreditLimit]  INT            NULL,
    [Blacklisted]  BIT            NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([CustomerNum] ASC)
);

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Product] (
    [ProductNum]  INT             NOT NULL,
    [Name]        NVARCHAR (50)   NULL,
    [Price]       DECIMAL (10, 2) NULL,
    [Stock]       INT             NULL,
    [Supplier]    NVARCHAR (50)   NULL,
    [Description] NVARCHAR (500)  NULL,
    [Expiry]      DATE            NULL,
    [Shelf]       INT             NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([ProductNum] ASC)
);

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Orders] (
    [OrderNum]        INT            NOT NULL,
    [CustomerNum]     INT            NULL,
    [DatePlace]       DATE           NULL,
    [DateShipped]     DATE           NULL,
    [DeliveryAddress] NVARCHAR (100) NULL,
    [Status]          NVARCHAR (20)  NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([OrderNum] ASC),
    FOREIGN KEY ([CustomerNum]) REFERENCES [dbo].[Customer] ([CustomerNum])
);

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[OrderItem] (
    [OrderItemNum] INT NOT NULL,
    [OrderNum]     INT NOT NULL,
    [ProductNum]   INT NULL,
    [Quantity]     INT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([OrderItemNum] ASC),
    FOREIGN KEY ([ProductNum]) REFERENCES [dbo].[Product] ([ProductNum]),
    FOREIGN KEY ([OrderNum]) REFERENCES [dbo].[Orders] ([OrderNum])
);
